-> User name

   UUID
   Publik key
   / A Hash of the Private key (No data can be recovered from this)

   Status

   / Reste token
   Created At
   Premium Status
   End of Premium time
->... ^krbthXdM

Organizes Omikrons
It saves and authenticates Omikron servers,
it also maps user IDs to the Omikron they are connected to:
-> User ID
   / Iota ID
   / Omikron ID -> when requested it will answer the IP:PORT/ARG
   User State (Online | Away | User offline ...)
-> ... ^WvXLhZWN

/ Marked information is not public ^9RdqACst

Sends messages between Clients & Iotas.
It assures privacy by anonymizing IP addresses.
It checks the authenticity of a connection 
( does a client provide valid credentials or is
  an Iota allowed to provide storage for a user )

-> / Iota ID
   / Iota connection
   -> User ID
      -> / User connection (Like your laptop)
      -> / User connection (Like your phone)
      -> ...
   -> ...
-> ... ^Bumztjk0

Client ^rSSi5aIF

Your active connection

The client is your primary interface
it gives you access to messaging and all other user features

You must provide your private key & your user id
In the web application you need to have a password manager
-> we advise Proton Pass

It stores your private key encrypted and uses the password manager to decrypt it.

Nothing stored in the client is public. ^8ikLwJVP

Iota ^WpDgBcQ9

Your local hosted server

It creates / deletes users
It stores the chats & communities.

Even though the iota stores your chats the administrator can only see who you are talking to but not the messages themselves.

On user creation you are provided a "<username>.pem" file this is your private key

ANYONE who has this file can access your account.
Store it on your own PC or a drive. ^u6vSe0rS
